<p>The <b>1999 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Youth_Championship" title="FIFA World Youth Championship">FIFA World Youth Championship</a></b> took place in <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> between April 3 and April 24, 1999. The 1999 championship was the 12th contested.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Squads">Squads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Squads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship_squads" title="1999 FIFA World Youth Championship squads">1999 FIFA World Youth Championship squads</a></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_stage">Group stage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Group stage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The 24 teams were split into six groups of four teams. Six group winners, six second-place finishers and the four best third-place finishers qualify for the knockout round.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_A">Group A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Group A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Round_of_16">Round of 16</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Round of 16">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final">Final</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1999_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Final">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
